msg:Today, I just came to Chengdu to see my friends. My friend lives on Tianfu 5th Street. I thought about booking a nearby hotel. I happened to eat Haidilao at the Grand Shopping Center. I found that there was a newly opened hotel next door.

There are now only three in China. The lobby is very spacious. There is a waterscape on the right side, which is quite beautiful. It is said to be the gate of Qingcheng Mountain, but there is a black head next to it, which is a bit strange.
The lobby is on the 19th floor. As soon as I got out of the elevator, I heard the sound of running water. I also joked whether it was leaking. As a result, there was a sound of running water in the waterscape by the window. It was quite innovative (the clown was myself!). The reflection of the mountain is a work of art. The young lady at the front desk said that this is the Qingcheng Mountain. The combination of landscape and water suddenly became awe-inspiring to the hotel designer.
The room is quite distinctive. Insert the power card in the door, and the light is on, the lid of a cylinder at the door rises, and there is music. When the lid is opened, a vinyl record is actually playing inside! ! ! Walking in from the door, the vaulted area in the middle is the dressing table, and then entering the bedroom is the bedroom. The dressing table also has a jewelry box (although I only have a pair of earrings...) In addition to the Fujia white beer, the other is some regular soft drinks. For L‚ÄôOccitane for washing, the sofa by the window seems to be a sofa bed.
The breakfast is quite normal, the tableware is quite unique, I like the color of the coffee cup very much, and the scenery outside the window is also good, but the weather is not so good, it can't be photographed.
